=== Greedy proof (diamond+SET+parity) ===
Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  SET: {row 5, row 6, row 8}РђЅРѕњРђЅ{col 3, col 6, col 9}.
      Remainder: {r6c8, r8c5} = {r9c6, r9c9}.
      Рєњ Both sides forced all-distinct. Virtual edges added.
  2.  SET: {row 5, row 6, row 9}РђЅРѕњРђЅ{col 3, col 6, col 9}.
      Remainder: {r6c8, r9c2} = {r8c3, r8c9}.
      Рєњ Both sides forced all-distinct. Virtual edges added.
  3.  Permutation fixpoint:
      row 5 {r5c3, r5c6, r5c9}
      row 6 {r6c3, r6c6, r6c8}
      row 8 {r8c3, r8c5, r8c9}
      row 9 {r9c2, r9c6, r9c9}
      Parallel links: row 5Рєћrow 6 (col, col, box); row 8Рєћrow 9 (box, box, col)
      All 6 pairs share a column Рєњ 4 distinct permutations.
      {row 5, row 6} same parity; {row 8, row 9} same parity.
      Only 3 per parity class Рєњ opposite classes.
      row 5 and row 8 share 2 columns: r5c3Рєћr8c3 (col 3), r5c9Рєћr8c9 (col 9).
      Opposite parity Рєњ relative permutation is a transposition.
      Fixpoint: color(r5c6) = color(r8c5). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {r5c9, r5c3, [r5c6=r8c5], r8c3} (spine r5c3Рђћ[r5c6=r8c5]).
      Рєњ color(r5c9) = color(r8c3). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {[r5c6=r8c5], r5c3, [r5c9=r8c3], r6c3} (spine r5c3Рђћ[r5c9=r8c3]).
      Рєњ color([r5c6=r8c5]) = color(r6c3). Identify.
  6.  Diamond {r5c3, [r5c6=r6c3=r8c5], [r5c9=r8c3], r6c8} (spine [r5c6=r6c3=r8c5]Рђћ[r5c9=r8c3]).
      Рєњ color(r5c3) = color(r6c8). Identify.

      row 5 {[r5c3=r6c8], [r5c6=r6c3=r8c5], [r5c9=r8c3]}
      row 6 {[r5c6=r6c3=r8c5], r6c6, [r5c3=r6c8]}
      row 8 {[r5c9=r8c3], [r5c6=r6c3=r8c5], r8c9}

      Рєњ same permutation parity.
      Each pair shares a column Рєњ distinct permutations.
      4 same-parity permutations from 3 available Рєњ pigeonhole contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. РќА

  1.  Diamond {r6c8, r4c9, r5c9, r9c9} (spine r4c9Рђћr5c9).
      Рєњ color(r6c8) = color(r9c9). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r6c6, r6c3, [r6c8=r9c9], r9c3} (spine r6c3Рђћ[r6c8=r9c9]).
      Рєњ color(r6c6) = color(r9c3). Identify.
  3.  SET: {row 8, row 9}РђЅРѕњРђЅ{box 8, box 9}.
      Remainder: {[r6c6=r9c3]} = {r7c6}.
      Рєњ color([r6c6=r9c3]) = color(r7c6), but they share a house. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. РќА
